1.3.2_personalized_predictions_standard

  • Show All Code
  • Hide All Code
Author

Saideep Gona

Published

November 22, 2023

Context

After training the Con-ENPACT model on variation in gene expression across the genome, it is good to also assess the accuracy on personalized variation. To do this, I can first generate Enformer predictions on the Aracena individuals I used for training.

Create list of individuals to predict on

Code

ind_counts = {}
for ind in vcf_inds:
    ind_counts[ind] = 0
    for exp_ind in individuals:
        if exp_ind in ind:
            ind_counts[ind] += 1


inds_pred = []
for ind in vcf_inds:
    if ind_counts[ind] == 1:
        inds_pred.append(ind)
    else:
        print(ind,ind_counts[ind])

print(inds_pred)

Code 
import pyliftover

lo = pyliftover.LiftOver('hg38', 'hg19')

tss_id_mapping = {}

lifted_over_tss = []
lifted_over_gene_ids = []
for gene_row in tss_meta_subset.iterrows():

    gene_chrom = "chr"+str(gene_row[1]["chromosome_name"])
    gene_tss = gene_row[1]["transcription_start_site"]
    # print(gene_row[1])
    try:
        gene_tss_hg19 = lo.convert_coordinate(gene_chrom,gene_tss)[0][1]
        lifted_over_tss.append(gene_chrom+"_"+str(gene_tss_hg19)+"_"+str(gene_tss_hg19+2))
        tss_id_mapping[gene_chrom+"_"+str(gene_tss_hg19)+"_"+str(gene_tss_hg19+2)] = gene_row[1]["ensembl_gene_id"]
        lifted_over_gene_ids.append(gene_row[1]["ensembl_gene_id"])
    except Exception as e:
        print(e)
        print(gene_chrom,gene_tss)
        continue

Split VCF by chrom

Collect results into singular table

Code 
import h5py

path_to_predictions = "/beagle3/haky/users/saideep/projects/aracena_modeling/enformer_predictions/aracena_preds/predictions_folder/enformer_aracena_preds_genes/predictions_2024-01-10/enformer_predictions"
collected_preds_dir = "/beagle3/haky/users/saideep/projects/aracena_modeling/enformer_predictions/aracena_preds/collected_preds"


for ind in inds_pred:
    predictions_dict_haplo1 = {}
    predictions_dict_haplo2 = {}
    print(ind)

    if os.path.exists(os.path.join(collected_preds_dir, ind+"_haplo1.txt")):
        if os.path.exists(os.path.join(collected_preds_dir, ind+"_haplo2.txt")):
            continue
    for i,gene_tss in enumerate(lifted_over_tss_towrite):
        pred_file_h1 = os.path.join(path_to_predictions,ind,"haplotype1",gene_tss+"_predictions.h5")
        pred_file_h2 = os.path.join(path_to_predictions,ind,"haplotype2",gene_tss+"_predictions.h5")
        if not (os.path.exists(pred_file_h1) and os.path.exists(pred_file_h2)):
            continue

        if not (os.path.exists(pred_file_h1) and os.path.exists(pred_file_h2)):
            print("missing",pred_file_h1,pred_file_h2)
            continue

        with h5py.File(pred_file_h1,"r") as f:
            pred_h1 = f[gene_tss][:]
            predictions_dict_haplo1[ind+"."+gene_tss] = pred_h1.mean(axis=0)
        with h5py.File(pred_file_h2,"r") as f:
            pred_h2 = f[gene_tss][:]
            predictions_dict_haplo2[ind+"."+gene_tss] = pred_h2.mean(axis=0)

    predictions_dict = pd.DataFrame(predictions_dict_haplo1).T
    print(predictions_dict.shape)
    predictions_dict.to_csv(os.path.join(collected_preds_dir, ind+"_haplo1.txt"),sep="\t")
    predictions_dict = pd.DataFrame(predictions_dict_haplo2).T
    predictions_dict.to_csv(os.path.join(collected_preds_dir, ind+"_haplo2.txt"),sep="\t")

Code 
predictions_dir = "/beagle3/haky/users/saideep/projects/aracena_modeling/enformer_predictions/aracena_preds/enpact_preds"

haplo1_preds_dfs = []
haplo2_preds_dfs = []
c=0
for ind in inds_pred:
    if not os.path.exists(os.path.join(predictions_dir,ind+"_haplo1_preds_RNAseq_Flu_personalized.txt")):
        continue
    if not os.path.exists(os.path.join(predictions_dir,ind+"_haplo2_preds_RNAseq_Flu_personalized.txt")):
        continue
    
    h1_cur = pd.read_csv(os.path.join(predictions_dir,ind+"_haplo1_preds_RNAseq_Flu_personalized.txt"),sep="\t",index_col=0)
    h2_cur = pd.read_csv(os.path.join(predictions_dir,ind+"_haplo2_preds_RNAseq_Flu_personalized.txt"),sep="\t",index_col=0)
    h1_cur.drop(index=h1_cur.index[0], axis=0, inplace=True)
    h2_cur.drop(index=h2_cur.index[0], axis=0, inplace=True)

    h1_cur["index_copy"] = h1_cur.index
    h1_cur[["ind","gene_region"]] = h1_cur["index_copy"].str.split('.', expand=True)
    h1_cur.index = h1_cur["gene_region"]
    h1_cur[ind] = h1_cur["lambda.min"]
    h1_cur.drop(columns=["index_copy","ind","gene_region","lambda.min"],inplace=True)

    h2_cur["index_copy"] = h2_cur.index
    h2_cur[["ind","gene_region"]] = h2_cur["index_copy"].str.split('.', expand=True)
    h2_cur.index = h2_cur["gene_region"]
    h2_cur[ind] = h2_cur["lambda.min"]
    h2_cur.drop(columns=["index_copy","ind","gene_region","lambda.min"],inplace=True)

    haplo1_preds_dfs.append(h1_cur)
    haplo2_preds_dfs.append(h2_cur)

    c+=1
    # if c==2:
    #     break
#
Code 
h1_full = pd.concat(haplo1_preds_dfs, join="inner", axis=1)

import seaborn as sns

corrs_Flu_permuted = matched_expression.corrwith(summed_haplos_permuted,axis=1,method="pearson")
corrs_Flu_permuted.hist(bins=100)

nullcorvec = np.tanh(np.random.normal(size=len(corrs_Flu))/np.sqrt(24-3))

for_hist_plot_df = pd.DataFrame({"Empirical":corrs_Flu,"Null":nullcorvec})
melted_df = for_hist_plot_df.melt(value_vars=["Empirical","Null"])
melted_df

sns.histplot(data=melted_df, x="value", hue="variable", bins=100)
plt.grid(False)
plt.xlabel("Pearson Correlation")
plt.ylabel("Count")
plt.title("Correlation distribution of Empirical(ENPACT) and Null")
plt.show()
plt.clf()

    melted_df.to_csv(os.path.join("/beagle3/haky/users/saideep/github_repos/Daily-Blog-Sai/posts/2023-11-22-retrain_expression_predictor","expression_personalized_corrs.csv"))

    print("Mean correlation across all genes, permuted:", corrs_Flu_permuted.mean())
    print("Variance of correlations across all genes, permuted:", corrs_Flu_permuted.var())

    sns.histplot(data=melted_df, x="value", hue="variable", bins=100)
    plt.grid(False)
    plt.xlabel("Pearson Correlation")
    plt.ylabel("Count")

This can also be examined by looking at enrichment over the null R2 distribution

Code 
def qqR2_python(pearson_r, nn, title="QQ Plot"):
    import numpy as np
    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
    ## nn is the sample size, number of individuals used to compute correlation.
    ## needs correlation vector as input.
    ## nullcorvec generates a random sample from correlation distributions, under the null hypothesis of 0 correlation using Fisher's approximation.
    corvec = pearson_r
    mm = len(corvec)
    nullcorvec = np.tanh(np.random.normal(size=mm)/np.sqrt(nn-3)) ## null correlation vector
    null_pearson_r = nullcorvec

    plt.plot(np.sort(null_pearson_r),np.sort(pearson_r),"o")
    plt.plot(pearson_r,pearson_r,"-")
    plt.xlabel("Null R")
    plt.ylabel("Empirical R")
    plt.title(title)
    plt.show()
    plt.clf()

    plt.plot(np.sort(null_pearson_r**2),np.sort(pearson_r**2),"o")
    plt.plot(pearson_r**2,pearson_r**2,"-")
    plt.xlabel("Null R2")
    plt.ylabel("Empirical R2")
    plt.title(title)
    plt.show()
    plt.clf()

# qqR2 = function(pearson_r,nn,pad_neg_with_0 = FALSE,...)
# {
# ## nn is the sample size, number of individuals used to compute correlation.
# ## needs correlation vector as input.
# ## nullcorvec generates a random sample from correlation distributions, under the null hypothesis of 0 correlation using Fisher's approximation.
#   corvec <- pearson_r
#   if(pad_neg_with_0) corvec[corvec < 0 | is.na(corvec) ]=0
#   mm <- length(corvec)
#   nullcorvec = tanh(rnorm(mm)/sqrt(nn-3)) ## null correlation vector
#   null_pearson_r <- nullcorvec
#   qqplot(null_pearson_r^2,pearson_r^2,...); abline(0,1); grid()
#   title(" ")
# }
Code 
qqR2_python(corrs_Flu,24,"Empirical(Enpact Predictions) vs. Null Correlation QQ Plot")

Probability that empirical mean is from null scrambling of individuals (check if there might be a bug with ordering of individuals)

Code 
permuted_means = []
permuted_vars = []
for i in range(100):
    if i%10==0:
        print(i)
    summed_haplos_permuted.columns = np.random.permutation(summed_haplos_permuted.columns)
    corrs_Flu_permuted = matched_expression.corrwith(summed_haplos_permuted,axis=1,method="spearman")
    permuted_means.append(corrs_Flu_permuted.mean())
    permuted_vars.append(corrs_Flu_permuted.var())

prop_greater_mean = sum([x>empirical_mean for x in permuted_means])/len(permuted_means)
print("Proportion of permuted means greater than empirical:", prop_greater_mean)
